The main host was Lee Jordan. ↵ The character names (and their code names) featured on the radio show include: ↵ Lee Jordan (code name: River) - The main host of the show. ↵ George Weasley (code name: Forge) - Ron Weasley's brother. ↵ Fred Weasley (code name: Gred) - George Weasley's brother. ↵ Remus Lupin (code name: Romulus) - A member of the Order of the Phoenix. ↵ Kingsley Shacklebolt (code name: Kingsley) - A Ministry of Magic official and Order member. ↵ Arthur Weasley - Mr. Weasley's voice was also heard on one broadcast (though a specific code name is not as widely noted as the others).
